########################
## Sichuan Focus Tree ##
## By Alpinia         ##
########################

focus_tree = {
	id = sichuan_focus
	country = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 10
			tag = SZC
		}
	}
	default = no
	continuous_focus_position = { x = 2600 y = 950 }

	shared_focus = SZC_Chengdu_Chongqing_Railway

	### Generic Post Unification ###
	shared_focus = CHS_provisional_government
	shared_focus = CHS_reintegrate_academies
	shared_focus = CHS_standardised_arsenals
	shared_focus = CHS_southern_fleets_legacy

	### Federalist Post Unification ###
	#Election related stuff
	shared_focus = UPC_affairs_of_the_ruling_coalition
	shared_focus = UPC_calls_for_a_constitutional_convention

	#Foreign Policy Tree
	shared_focus = CHN_return_to_the_world_stage_focus

	### Table of Contents ###
	# Economic Tree

	# Shared Military Tree
	# Zhili Military Tree
	# Baoding/Officer Department Military Tree
	# Accelerated Military Tree

	# Armament Political Focus Tree
	# Baoding Department Political Tree
	# Accelerated Department Political Tree
	# Officer Department Focus Tree
	# Federalist Bastion Tree
	# Zhili Remnant Tree

### Shared Military Tree ###
	focus = {
		id = SZC_Rebuild_The_Sichuanese_Army
		icon = GFX_goal_break_rifle
		cost = 5

		x = 25
		y = 0

		available = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = SZC_internal_divisions }
				NOT = { has_idea = SZC_internal_divisions }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = SZC_civil_war_idea }
				NOT = { has_idea = SZC_civil_war_idea }
			}
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_country_leader = { character = SZC_liu_xiang }
						has_country_leader = { character = SZC_power_vacuum }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		offset = {
			x = -1
			y = 0
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = SZC_baoding_department_in_power
					has_country_flag = SZC_officer_department_in_power
				}
			}
		}
		offset = {
			x = -18
			y = 0
			trigger = {
				has_country_flag = SZC_federalists_in_power
			}
		}
		offset = {
			x = -3
			y = 0
			trigger = {
				has_country_flag = SZC_accelerated_department_in_power
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				has_war = yes
			}
		}
		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Focus Completed SZC_Rebuild_The_Sichuanese_Army"
			army_experience = 25
			add_war_support = 0.05
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ARMY_XP }
	}

	focus = {
		id = SZC_Rebuild_The_Officer_Corps
		icon = GFX_focus_generic_military_academy
		cost = 5

		relative_position_id = SZC_Rebuild_The_Sichuanese_Army
		x = 4
		y = 0

		available = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = SZC_internal_divisions }

				name = SZC_Rebuild_The_Officer_Corps

		}

	}

	focus = {

### Zhili Military Tree ###
	focus = {
		id = SZC_Adopt_The_Southern_Doctrine
		icon = GFX_goal_SZC_southern_doctrine
		cost = 5

		relative_position_id = SZC_Rebuild_The_Sichuanese_Army
		x = 0
		y = 2

		allow_branch = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = SZC_armament_department_in_power
				has_country_flag = SZC_zhili_exiles_in_power
			}
		}
		mutually_exclusive = {
			focus = SZC_Continue_The_Northern_Doctrine
		}
		prerequisite = {
			focus = SZC_New_Infantry_Weapons
		}
		prerequisite = {
			focus = SZC_Recon_Unit_Training
		}
		prerequisite = {
			focus = SZC_Mountain_Warfare
		}
		prerequisite = {
			focus = SZC_Import_Modern_Artillery
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				has_war = yes
			}
		}
		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Focus Completed SZC_Adopt_The_Southern_Doctrine"
			add_ideas = SZC_southern_doctrine_1
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ARMY_BONUS }
	}

	focus = {
		id = SZC_War_Logistics
		icon = GFX_goal_generic_war_in_the_plate
		cost = 5

		relative_position_id = SZC_Rebuild_The_Sichuanese_Army
		x = -1
		y = 4

		prerequisite = {
			focus = SZC_Adopt_The_Southern_Doctrine
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				has_war = yes
			}
		}
		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Focus Completed SZC_War_Logistics"
			if = { #has better unit org
				limit = { has_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_3 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_3
					add_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_4
				}
			}
			else_if = { #has heavy fire tactics
				limit = { has_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_5 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_5
					add_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_7
				}
			}
			else_if = { #has increased munitions production
				limit = { has_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_6 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_6
					add_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_6
				}
			}
			else_if = { #has heavy fire tactics and increased munitions production
				limit = { has_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_9 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_9
					add_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_10
				}
			}
			else = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_1
					add_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_2
				}
			}
			every_army_leader = {
				add_logistics = 1
			}
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ARMY_BONUS }
	}

				}

					remove_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_4
					add_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_7
				}
			}
			else_if = { #has increased munitions production

				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_6
					add_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_9
				}
			}
			else_if = { #has war logistics and increased munitions production
				limit = { has_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_8 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_8
					add_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_10
				}
			}
			else_if = { #has focus on speed
				limit = { has_idea = SZC_northern_doctrine_2 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SZC_northern_doctrine_2
					add_idea = SZC_northern_doctrine_5
				}
			}
			else_if = { #has focus on speed and improved army training
				limit = { has_idea = SZC_northern_doctrine_4 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SZC_northern_doctrine_4
					add_idea = SZC_northern_doctrine_8
				}
			}
			else_if = { #has increased munitions production
				limit = { has_idea = SZC_northern_doctrine_6 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SZC_northern_doctrine_6
					add_idea = SZC_northern_doctrine_7
				}
			}
			else_if = { #has increased munitions production and improved army training
				limit = { has_idea = SZC_northern_doctrine_9 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SZC_northern_doctrine_9
					add_idea = SZC_northern_doctrine_10
				}
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = {
					localization_key = tooltip_modify_two_dynmods
					DYNMOD1 = SZC_southern_doctrine
					DYNMOD2 = SZC_northern_doctrine
				}
				effect_tooltip = {
					add_to_temp_variable = {
						army_attack_factor = 0.1
						tooltip = army_attack_factor_tooltip
					}
				}
			}
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ARMY_BONUS }
	}

				}
			}
			else_if = { #has heavy fire tactics and increased munitions production
				limit = { has_idea = SZC_northern_doctrine_7 }

	focus = {
		id = SZC_Dedicated_Logistics_Units
		icon = GFX_goal_generic_construction2
		cost = 5

		relative_position_id = SZC_Army_Drills
		x = -3
		y = 2

		prerequisite = {
			focus = SZC_Adopt_Radio_Communications
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				has_war = yes
			}
		}
		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Focus Completed SZC_Dedicated_Logistics_Units"
			if = { #has operations
				limit = { has_idea = SZC_industrial_army_2 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SZC_industrial_army_2
					add_idea = SZC_industrial_army_5
				}
			}
			else_if = { #has firepower
				limit = { has_idea = SZC_industrial_army_3 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SZC_industrial_army_3
					add_idea = SZC_industrial_army_6
				}
			}
			else_if = { #has production
				limit = { has_idea = SZC_industrial_army_4 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SZC_industrial_army_4
					add_idea = SZC_industrial_army_7
				}
			}
			else_if = { #has operations and firepower
				limit = { has_idea = SZC_industrial_army_8 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SZC_industrial_army_8
					add_idea = SZC_industrial_army_11
				}
			}
			else_if = { #has operations and production
				limit = { has_idea = SZC_industrial_army_9 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SZC_industrial_army_9
					add_idea = SZC_industrial_army_12
				}
			}
			else_if = { #has firepower and production
				limit = { has_idea = SZC_industrial_army_10 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SZC_industrial_army_10
					add_idea = SZC_industrial_army_13
